<p><strong>74:46</strong> — وَكُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َا نُكَذِّبُ بِيَوۡمِ ٱلدِّينِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:50</strong> — كَأَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َهُمۡ حُمُرٌ مُّسۡتَنفِرَةٌ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:54</strong> — كَلَّآ إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َهُۥ تَذۡكِرَةٌ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:2</strong> — وَلَآ أُقۡسِمُ بِٱل<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َفۡسِ ٱللَّوَّامَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:17</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ عَلَيۡنَا جَمۡعَهُۥ وَقُرۡءَانَهُۥ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:19</strong> — ثُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َ إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ عَلَيۡنَا بَيَانَهُۥ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:25</strong> — تَظُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>ُ أَن يُفۡعَلَ بِهَا فَاقِرَةٌ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:28</strong> — وَظَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ أَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َهُ ٱلۡفِرَاقُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:33</strong> — ثُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َ ذَهَبَ إِلَىٰٓ أَهۡلِهِۦ يَتَمَطَّىٰٓ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:35</strong> — ثُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َ أَوۡلَىٰ لَكَ فَأَوۡلَىٰٓ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:38</strong> — ثُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َ كَانَ عَلَقَةً فَخَلَقَ فَسَوَّىٰ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:2</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َا خَلَقۡنَا ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ مِن نُّطۡفَةٍ أَمۡشَاجٍ نَّبۡتَلِيهِ فَجَعَلۡنَـٰهُ سَمِيعَۢا بَصِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:3</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َا هَدَيۡنَـٰهُ ٱلسَّبِيلَ إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َا شَاكِرًا وَإِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َا كَفُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 3)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:4</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َآ أَعۡتَدۡنَا لِلۡكَـٰفِرِينَ سَلَـٰسِلَاۡ وَأَغۡلَـٰلاً وَسَعِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:5</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ ٱلۡأَبۡرَارَ يَشۡرَبُونَ مِن كَأۡسٍ كَانَ مِزَاجُهَا كَافُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:7</strong> — يُوفُونَ بِٱل<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َذۡرِ وَيَخَافُونَ يَوۡمًا كَانَ شَرُّهُۥ مُسۡتَطِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:9</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َمَا نُطۡعِمُكُمۡ لِوَجۡهِ ٱللَّهِ لَا نُرِيدُ مِنكُمۡ جَزَآءً وَلَا شُكُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:10</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َا نَخَافُ مِن رَّبِّنَا يَوۡمًا عَبُوسًا قَمۡطَرِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:12</strong> — وَجَزَٮٰهُم بِمَا صَبَرُواۡ جَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َةً وَحَرِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:18</strong> — عَيۡنًا فِيهَا تُسَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َىٰ سَلۡسَبِيلاً <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:20</strong> — وَإِذَا رَأَيۡتَ ثَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َ رَأَيۡتَ نَعِيمًا وَمُلۡكًا كَبِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:22</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ هَـٰذَا كَانَ لَكُمۡ جَزَآءً وَكَانَ سَعۡيُكُم مَّشۡكُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:23</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا عَلَيۡكَ ٱلۡقُرۡءَانَ تَنزِيلاً <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:27</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ هَـٰٓؤُلَآءِ يُحِبُّونَ ٱلۡعَاجِلَةَ وَيَذَرُونَ وَرَآءَهُمۡ يَوۡمًا ثَقِيلاً <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:29</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ هَـٰذِهِۦ تَذۡكِرَةٌ‌ۖ فَمَن شَآءَ ٱتَّخَذَ إِلَىٰ رَبِّهِۦ سَبِيلاً <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:30</strong> — وَمَا تَشَآءُونَ إِلَّآ أَن يَشَآءَ ٱللَّهُ‌ۚ إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ ٱللَّهَ كَانَ عَلِيمًا حَكِيمًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:3</strong> — وَٱل<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َـٰشِر<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>تِ نَشۡرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:7</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َمَا تُوعَدُونَ لَو<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>قِعٌ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:8</strong> — فَإِذَا ٱل<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>ُجُومُ طُمِسَتۡ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:17</strong> — ثُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َ نُتۡبِعُهُمُ ٱلۡأَخِرِينَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:32</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َهَا تَرۡمِى بِشَرَرٍ كَٱلۡقَصۡرِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:33</strong> — كَأَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َهُۥ جِمَـٰلَتٌ صُفۡرٌ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:41</strong> — إِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>نّ</span>َ ٱلۡمُتَّقِينَ فِى ظِلَـٰلٍ وَعُيُونٍ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:42</strong> — وَفَو<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>كِهَ مِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>مّ</span>َا يَشۡتَهُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
